 chapter 1 trip was late .

 *** we started up the trail toward the cave just past six , after picking up tannis at her house a half mile from mine and natalie at the ski shop . 
 it was near dusk , but none of us needed much light to find our way . 
 we 'd been doing it all summer .

 he and i were going hunting .

 chapter 27 there are three cemetaries in buford . 
 my dad was buried in the one farthest from our house . 
 i would n't have minded if it were across the country .

 he 'd broken one of his cardinal rules and hunted alone .
